Diplomatic edition of London ms. BL Add ms 12277

Authors of digital edition: Arlo Griffiths & Nurmalia Habibah

Filename: Fill in the filename with the xml extension

Language: Undetermined

Repository: Nusantara Philology (tfd-nusantara-philology)

Version: part commented since without access_token with github actions api calls are limited – still working on it

Witness

  • Leiden, University Library (UB), Lontar, Or. 23732
    • Content:
      • Vipañcitārthā by Śāntarakṣita
    • Physical Description: Palm-leaf manuscript. 89 leaves in Kuṭilā script. Apparently written in 1152 A.C.
    • Hand Description: A1:H1 main hand of the manuscript, black ink, Sundanese script
    • History: In June 1934, Sāṅkṛtyāyana found this manuscript in the monastery of Kun-de-ling (Lhasa).
